# CSM-WA Workarounds - Errores de producción CSM
# Archivo generado desde lista de workarounds del equipo

[ERROR]
SC_ENV Error - "sc_env" routine failed to handle the transaction receive from CSM

[DESCRIPTION]
This error happens when there is no entry on nbi_mdn table.

[WORKAROUND]
Check if there is entry or not:

select * from nbi_mdn where subscriber_no='&sub';

Use below script to insert entry on nbi_mdn:
@inbi

1  accept ctn prompt "Please enter CTN/Subscriber_No:"
2  DEFINE sub = &sub
3  prompt "Get to most recent date"
4  select INIT_REQ_DATE,port_path,request_sts from port_request where request_no in (select request_no from sub_port_request where subscriber_no='&sub');
5  select related_market from market where market_code in (select distinct sub_market_code from npa_nxx_vh where npa||nxx=substr('&sub',1,6));
6  insert into nbi_mdn values('&sub','&date',null,null,null,'WLNP',null,'&mkt',null);
7  commit;
8* UNDEFINE sub

[TAGS]
SC_ENV, nbi_mdn, port, CSM

[ERROR]
Ban in use

[DESCRIPTION]
Error when BAN is locked due to reprice request status.

[TUXEDO_ERROR]
-------------------------------------------------
--- Error logged at: 08:03:36
--- Stack Id: csmUFoldr #3
--------------------------------------------------
1) Msg:  Get SUBSCRIBER row for customer_id: 392026301691, subscriber_no: 9182240443 has failed
  Code: DCS_SUBSCR_GT_FAILURE, C8CE0174 User Value: 0
  File: dcs_subscr.c Line: 72958  (dcs_gt_all_sn_info_by_sub)
2) Msg: ORA-01410: invalid ROWID
  Code: , -1410 User Value: 0
  File: dcs_subscr.c Line: 72958  (dcs_gt_all_sn_info_by_sub)
3) Msg: Trace Failure
  Code: ERR_TRACE_FAILURE, 80000005 User Value: 4
  File: /opt/app/cchome/ccsbms/bb/sbmscs Line: 9823  (cvRollback)
4) Msg: Trace Failure
  Code: ERR_TRACE_FAILURE, 80000005 User Value: 4
  File: /opt/app/cchome/ccsbms/bb/sbmscs Line: 29217  (cvSvBanFldr)
5) Msg: Trace Failure
  Code: ERR_TRACE_FAILURE, 80000005 User Value: 4
  File: /opt/app/cchome/ccsbms/bb/sbmscs Line: 679  (pcsi_gt_lock_type_and_lock_inter)
6) Msg: Trace Failure
  Code: ERR_TRACE_FAILURE, 80000005 User Value: 4
  File: /opt/app/cchome/ccsbms/bb/sbmscs Line: 1353  (pcsi_perform_locking_internal)
7) Msg: BAN  (392026301691) in use. Please try accessing account again later.
  Code: CSMPL_BAN_LOCKED, 0 User Value: 0
  File: /opt/app/cchome/ccsbms/bb/sbmscs Line: 791  (pcsi_sub_mem_grp_lk)

[WORKAROUND]
1. If there is an error for ban in use (7):
select reprice_sts, count(*) from llp_reprice_request where ban=&ban group by reprice_sts;

R|        COUNT(*)
-|----------------
C|               8
S|               1

2. If any in F status change them to L to resolve ban in use:
update llp_reprice_request set reprice_sts='L' where reprice_sts='F' and ban=&ban;
Commit changes

3. If the above work around doesn't work please try the below one:

/*This scripts changes the allow concurrent users under locking mechanism*/
accept ban prompt "Please enter BAN: " default 10
select cs_lock_mechanism from billing_account where ban = &ban;
update billing_account set cs_lock_mechanism='L' where ban = &ban;
select cs_lock_mechanism from billing_account where ban = &ban;
undefine ban

[TAGS]
csmUFoldr, ban in use, llp_reprice_request, billing_account

[ERROR]
Number of rows exceeds buffer's capacity

[DESCRIPTION]
This happens when there are a lot of entries on service_agreement table for one BAN and CTN/Subscriber_No.

[WORKAROUND]
Use the below script to remove expired entries on service_agreement:

SQL> !cat rm_exp_soc.sql
-- This script will delete SOCS in SA and SF tables
prompt "This script will list all the similar SOCS in SA and SF tables"
accept ctn prompt "Please enter CTN/Subscriber_No: "
accept ban prompt "Please enter BAN: "

--backup all data from SA and SF
create table sa_bkp_&ctn as select * from SERVICE_AGREEMENT where subscriber_no='&ctn' and ban=&ban;
create table sf_bkp_&ctn as select * from SERVICE_FEATURE where subscriber_no='&ctn' and ban=&ban;
grant select on sa_bkp_&ctn to public;
grant select on sf_bkp_&ctn to public;

--expire SOCs
delete SERVICE_FEATURE where subscriber_no in ('&ctn') and ban in ('&ban') and ftr_expiration_date is not null;
delete service_agreement where subscriber_no in ('&ctn') and ban in ('&ban') and expiration_date is not null;

undefine ban
undefine ctn

[TAGS]
service_agreement, service_feature, buffer, SA, SF

---

[ERROR]
NPAC

[DESCRIPTION]
This error happens when the port request last status_act is not NOTG and doesn't let execute the number change/activation.

[WORKAROUND]
Execute the below scripts and use the request number and last act_seq_no from that request:
@npacu

1  accept REQUEST_NO prompt "Please enter REQUEST_NO: "
2  select REQUEST_NO,ACT_SEQ_NO,resp_type,action_id,action_status from act_port_request
3  where REQUEST_NO in ('&REQUEST_NO') order by ACT_SEQ_NO asc;
4  update act_port_request set ACTION_ID='NOTG' where REQUEST_NO ='&REQUEST_NO' and ACT_SEQ_NO='&ACT_SEQ_NO';
5* undefine REQUEST_NO

[TAGS]
NPAC, act_port_request, port, NOTG, number change

[ERROR]
Cannot invoke Web service: salesChannel Is/Are Required

[DESCRIPTION]
Unable to resume from cancel. When attempting to resume in Telegence, the system spins for a very long time with blue circle and then the Ban closes.
Example: customer has had no service since 9/12/25, CTN 916-718-0798. No explicit ERROR shown.

[WORKAROUND]
1. Check Records:
select ban,CH_CRSM_ON_OFF_IND from credit_history where ban=&ban and CH_CRSM_ON_OFF_IND = 'Y';

2. Backup Records:
create table c_h_bkp_clf as select * from credit_history where ban=&ban and CH_CRSM_ON_OFF_IND = 'Y';

3. Update Records:
update credit_history set CH_CRSM_ON_OFF_IND = 'N' where ban=&ban and CH_CRSM_ON_OFF_IND = 'Y';

4. Commit Changes:
commit;

[TAGS]
salesChannel, resume from cancel, credit_history, Telegence, CH_CRSM_ON_OFF_IND

[ERROR]
Error after calling aram_res_promo_credits / GnDts_MonthsDiff - ORA-00100 no data found

[DESCRIPTION]
Multiple errors preventing desired action:
1) Error after calling aram_res_promo_credits, returned status: -1
2) Error after calling GnDts_MonthsDiff, returned status: -1
3) Non digit in parameter datetime
4) ORA-00100: no data found
5) ORA-00100: no data found

[WORKAROUND]
SQL> @aram_promo

This Script fixes the above errors.

Please enter CTN/Subscriber_No and BAN when prompted.

Steps performed by script:
- create table cp_&ban as select * from cpc_promos where subscriber_no='&ctn' and ban=&ban
- grant all on cp_&ban to public
- select from cpc_promos where ban=&ban and SUBSCRIBER_NO='&ctn' order by PROMO_SEQ_NO
- Enter SYS_CREATION_DATE from bigger PROMO_SEQ_NO (YYYY-MM-DD) to assign to previous record with null date (there must be only 1 rec with null NCD)
- update cpc_promos set NEXT_CREDIT_DATE=to_date('&NCD_yyyy_mm_dd','yyyy-mm-dd') where ban=&ban and SUBSCRIBER_NO='&ctn' and PROMO_SEQ_NO='&PROMO_SEQ_NO'
- Verify with select and commit

Example:
update cpc_promos set NEXT_CREDIT_DATE=to_date('2026-MAR-06','yyyy-mm-dd') where ban=287364215492 and SUBSCRIBER_NO='9255672021' and PROMO_SEQ_NO='21371232';
commit;

[TAGS]
aram_res_promo_credits, GnDts_MonthsDiff, cpc_promos, ORA-00100, promo credits

[ERROR]
This installment plan cannot be reinstated because the current contract is not installment related. A new installment plan must be created.

[DESCRIPTION]
Last entry of contract should be EMR, the previous must be PPD.

[TUXEDO_ERROR]
Please move the Installment/EMR contract 08/11/24 for 405 996 0198 to the top so it can be reinstated.
 
Trying to reinstate the IP 320000006309968 and receive:
 
---------------------------
Reinstate ineligible (#802855)
---------------------------
This installment plan cannot be reinstated because the current contract is not installment related. A new installment plan must be created.
---------------------------
OK   
---------------------------

[WORKAROUND]
FOLLOW THE BELOW EXAMPLE:

--CHECK CONTRACT TABLE AND LOOK FOR THE LATEST ENTRY
SQL> @con
Enter value for ban: 133034226376
Enter value for sub: 8707232637

select item_id,CNT_SEQ_NO,EFFECTIVE_DATE,COMMIT_START_DATE,COMMIT_END_DATE,COMMIT_ORIG_NO_MONTH,ELIGIBILITY_RESULT,RSN_CODE,LAST_UPGRADE_DATE,COMMIT_REASON_CD,TC_APPROVAL_REQ,parked_cont_reason,CONTRACT_GRP_CD,XUPG_SEQ_NO,DF_STATUS,upg_rev_date,upg_rev_rsn_cd from contract where ban=&ban and subscriber_no='&sub';

-- COMMIT_REASON_CD MUST BE 'EMR' on latest entry. In failing cases it shows 'PPD'.

--Create a bkp
create table contract_8707232637 as select * from contract where ban=133034226376 and subscriber_no='8707232637';

--Update latest to EMR, set others with same date to PPD so they don't cause interference
update contract set COMMIT_REASON_CD='EMR' where ban=133034226376 and subscriber_no='8707232637' and CNT_SEQ_NO=222932511;
update contract set COMMIT_REASON_CD='PPD' where ban=133034226376 and subscriber_no='8707232637' and COMMIT_REASON_CD='EMR' and CNT_SEQ_NO in (221439687,222924117,222924119,222924121);

commit;

[TAGS]
installment plan, contract, EMR, PPD, COMMIT_REASON_CD

[ERROR]
CANCEL CTN - ERR_TRACE_FAILURE (csCnclSub / arCnclBan)

[DESCRIPTION]

On contract table there was no record for active IMEI (350255144268840).

[TUXEDO_ERROR]
--------------------------------------------------
--- Error logged at: 12:26:38
--- Stack Id: csmUBanAct #1
--------------------------------------------------

1) Msg: Trace Failure
  Code: ERR_TRACE_FAILURE, 80000005 User Value: 4
  File: /opt/app/cchome/ccsbms/bb/sbmscs Line: 801  (arCnclBan)
  
2) Msg: Trace Failure
  Code: ERR_TRACE_FAILURE, 80000005 User Value: 4
  File: /opt/app/cchome/ccsbms/bb/sbmscs Line: 3191  (par_cancle_ban_func)
  
3) Msg: Trace Failure
  Code: ERR_TRACE_FAILURE, 80000005 User Value: 4
  File: /opt/app/cchome/ccsbms/bb/sbmscs Line: 8000  (csCnclSub)
  
4) Msg: Trace Failure
  Code: ERR_TRACE_FAILURE, 80000005 User Value: 4
  File: /opt/app/cchome/ccsbms/bb/sbmscs Line: 171  (pcs_handle_stolen_in_transit_cas)


[WORKAROUND]
@pdev

Check physical_device entries for subscriber.

@con

Check contract entries for subscriber.

-- Need to create an entry on contract table for ITEM_ID=PDA09811, IMEI=350255144268840

create table contract_6293269460 as select * from contract where ban=545204989042 and subscriber_no='6293269460' and ITEM_ID='PDA10130';

-- Change record in order to match with current IMEI
update contract_6293269460 set ITEM_ID='PDA09811',sys_creation_date=to_date('2026-04-20 17:34:07', 'yyyy-mm-dd hh24:mi:ss'),
CNT_SEQ_NO=contract_1sq.nextval, effective_date=to_date('2026-04-20','yyyy-mm-dd'),imei='350255144268840';

-- INSERT NEW ENTRY ON CONTRACT TABLE
insert into contract select * from contract_6293269460;

-- If CTN already canceled, remove duplicate entry:
delete from contract where ban=545204989042 and subscriber_no='6293269460' and item_id='PDA09811';

[TAGS]
CANCEL CTN, ERR_TRACE_FAILURE, csCnclSub, contract, IMEI, physical_device

[ERROR]
NUMBER CHANGE

[DESCRIPTION]
Buffer issue for too many records in act_port_request table.
Error: We receive error "csChgSub00 failed. Tuxedo error TPESVCERRserver error
while handling request 10" while doing a number change

[WORKAROUND]
We should no longer manipulate the port request records, just ask the user to open a new port request.

In case there is no other option, for a quick fix remove all entries but the last 5 and retry the activity:

-- act_port_request
create table apr_bkp_12135077 as select * from act_port_request where request_no=12135077;
delete from act_port_request where request_no=12135077 and act_seq_no < 125040592;
insert into act_port_request select * from apr_bkp_12135077 where request_no=12135077 and act_seq_no < 125040592;

-- sub_port_request
create table spr_bkp_12135077 as select * from sub_port_request where request_no=12135077;
delete from sub_port_request where request_no=12135077 and act_seq_no < 125040592;
insert into sub_port_request select * from spr_bkp_12135077 where request_no=12135077 and act_seq_no < 125040592;

-- sub_port_resp
create table spre_bkp_12135077 as select * from sub_port_resp where request_no=12135077;
delete from sub_port_resp where request_no=12135077;
insert into sub_port_resp select * from spre_bkp_12135077;

[TAGS]
number change, csChgSub00, TPESVCERR, act_port_request, sub_port_request, buffer

[ERROR]
RESUME

[DESCRIPTION]
SUB_STATUS_DATE is more than 3 months old

Mkt: GLF
Ban: 578124533936
Ctn: 2517698030
Request: Please resume ctn 2517698030 on ban 578124533936
Error: We receive error "Resume is not a valid activity." while resuming the ctn

Resume is not a valid activity since SUB_STATUS_DATE is more than 3 months old,
so fix is to update subscriber, SA, SF, SAH and phisical_devices tables with a recent date

[WORKAROUND]
script: allow_resume.sql
-- SQL to update specific dates to allow resume, since cancelation date must be less than 30 days old
accept ctn prompt "Please enter CTN/Subscriber_No: "
accept ban prompt "Please enter BAN: "
select to_char(SUB_STATUS_DATE,'yyyy-mm-dd') from subscriber where subscriber_no='&ctn' and customer_ban=&ban;
accept date prompt "Please enter original SUB_STATUS_DATE (yyyy-mm-dd): "

update subscriber set SUB_STATUS_DATE=trunc(sysdate-10),APPLICATION_ID='CLARIF',
DL_SERVICE_CODE=substr(user,1,5) where subscriber_no='&ctn' and customer_ban=&ban;
update physical_device set expiration_date=trunc(sysdate-10),application_id='CLARIF',
DL_SERVICE_CODE=substr(user,1,5) where CUSTOMER_ID='&ban' and subscriber_no='&ctn'
and trunc(expiration_date)=trunc(to_date('&date','yyyy-mm-dd'));
update service_agreement set expiration_date=trunc(sysdate-10),APPLICATION_ID='CLARIF',
DL_SERVICE_CODE=substr(user,1,5) where subscriber_no='&ctn' and ban=&ban
and trunc(expiration_date)=trunc(to_date('&date','yyyy-mm-dd'));
update SERVICE_FEATURE set ftr_expiration_date=trunc(sysdate-10),APPLICATION_ID='CLARIF',
DL_SERVICE_CODE=substr(user,1,5) where subscriber_no='&ctn' and ban=&ban
and trunc(ftr_expiration_date)=trunc(to_date('&date','yyyy-mm-dd'));
update srv_agr_history set new_exp_date=trunc(sysdate-10),
history_issue_date=trunc(sysdate-10),APPLICATION_ID='CLARIF',DL_SERVICE_CODE=substr(user,1,5)
where subscriber_no= '&ctn' and ban='&ban' and trunc(NEW_EXP_DATE)=trunc(to_date('&date','yyyy-mm-dd'));
 
undefine date
undefine ban
undefine ctn

2nd update option in case S_A_H error
update srv_agr_history set RC_EXP_RSN_CODE='T',new_exp_date=to_date('20210505','yyyymmdd'),
history_issue_date=to_date('20210505','yyyymmdd') where subscriber_no='2517698030'
and ban='578124533936' and RC_EXP_RSN_CODE='Z';

@rm_exp_soc
--Backup all data from SA and SF
create table sa_bkp_&ctn as select * from SERVICE_AGREEMENT where subscriber_no='&ctn' and ban=&ban;
create table sf_bkp_&ctn as select * from SERVICE_FEATURE where subscriber_no='&ctn' and ban=&ban;

delete service_agreement where subscriber_no='&ctn' and ban='&ban' and expiration_date<sysdate;

@in_exp_soc
insert into service_agreement select * from sa_bkp_&ctn where expiration_date < sysdate;
insert into service_feature select * from sf_bkp_&ctn where ftr_expiration_date < sysdate;

[WORKAROUND]
There is a common case where the user moves/changes the subscriber and 
then tries to do a resume instead of adding the CTN as a new subscriber, this
leaves three possible problems:
- Leaves the duplicate mnet_subid

Subscriber Number : 9453540554 
Market : DLS 
Timestamp: 25-AUG-25 09:10:21 EST 
 
Issue Description :
TLG has sent multiple DEFAULT_DNN values in a single transaction. This violates 
the system constraint that allows only one DEFAULT_DNN value,
 with a maximum length of 50 characters. The breach has led to data exceeding the

[ERROR]
Unable to active parked equipment due to duplicate active socs

[DESCRIPTION]
Request: WR#4680806
I have a customer that is not able to activate parked equipment.
When we attempted in OPUS we get error saying SOC IPME already exists.
I also get the same error when i attempted in TLG.
We have tried to delete parked equipment and we encounter same issue.
I believe it has to do with a future dated rate plan set for 10/9/2025, I attempted to change that and not able to.  

Can you please help remove what is causing us from activating customers parked equipment so they can start using new phone.   
BAN:392017734421 
CTN: 9183131715 
AOTS Ticket # 335937920

[WORKAROUND]
1. Identify the duplicate socs
select soc, count(*) from service_agreement where ban=392017734421 and subscriber_no='9183131715'
and expiration_date is null group by soc having count(*) > 1;
select subscriber_no,soc,soc_effective_date,effective_date,expiration_date,rc_eff_rsn_code,
rc_exp_rsn_code,service_type,rel_soc,REL_SOC_SEQ_NO,glpp_id,srv_ftr_ind,soc_seq_no,soc_ver_no,
agr_parking_ind,agr_enabler_ind from service_agreement where ban=392017734421 and subscriber_no='9183131715' and soc like '%IPME%';
2. Backup the socs to expire
select count(*) from sa_bkp_wr;
create table sa_bkp_wr as select * from service_agreement where soc_seq_no='232724052' and subscriber_no='9183131715' and ban=392017734421;
insert into sa_bkp_wr select * from service_agreement where soc_seq_no='232724052' and subscriber_no='9183131715' and ban=392017734421;
3. Expire socs
update service_agreement set expiration_date=sysdate-1 where soc_seq_no='232724052' and subscriber_no='9183131715' and ban=392017734421;

 CUSTOMER_ID|W|WAL_EFF_DATETIME   |WAL_EXP_DATETIME|OTHER_TELN|OTHER_TN_TYPE
------------|-|-------------------|----------------|----------|-------------
534240167899|Y|2026-02-03 22:05:58|                |          |
    
GLR
 CUSTOMER_ID|W|WAL_EFF_DATETIME   |WAL_EXP_DATETIME|OTHER_TELN|OTHER_TN_TYPE
------------|-|-------------------|----------------|----------|-------------
188081968483|Y|2026-02-01 18:26:37|                |          |

- WAL_IND related issues (Wireless Account Lock)
For any future request regarding to WAL status on our side (could be remove or add)
please engage Willis Charisma G (cw136g)/MICHAEL, LINSLEY lm1254@att.com,
explain the request and only perform the updates with her approval.
Since this is a security mechanism implemented by business we need their approval
for any change from backend.

Error (#803390) 
AT&T Wireless Account Lock is enabled on this account.  Instruct the customer to
go to myAT&T app and toggle OFF AT&T Wireless Account Lock to proceed with this
transaction"

To check WAL status:
select customer_id, wal_ind, wal_eff_datetime, wal_exp_datetime, other_telno,
other_tn_type from customer where customer_id='&ban';
To remove WAL:
create table cus_&ban as select * from customer where customer_id=&ban;
update customer set wal_ind=null, wal_eff_datetime=null where customer_id=&ban;
To set WAL:
update customer set wal_ind='Y', wal_eff_datetime=sysdate where customer_id=&ban;
Please remember that any WAL activity will create BAN level memos
(when they are done by any FE, and no memos if we update in backend)
WAL_IND = Null means thar WAL has NEVER been updated for the BAN
WAL_IND = ‘Y’ means thar WAL is AVTIVE for the BAN (No changes allowed)
WAL_IND = ‘N’ means thar WAL has been updated from Y to N for the BAN

Linsley team is: Customer Protection & Risk Management (CPRM) PMO

Move FN IND & Type Back to BAN Level for FN Sub Paid 3PT Acct

[DESCRIPTION]
Request: WR#4735910
We have a FirstNet subscriber paid account in Guam (BAN 337251440729, CTN 6199638360,
that was inappropriately activated to stateside FirstNet & Family. I will be
updating the FAN and rate plan, but I need the FN indicator and type (V1) to be
set back to the BAN level instead of the CTN level, so that the account acts
like a "legacy" subscriber paid account and not a FirstNet & Family account. 
Canek resolved a similar issue in WR #4430466. Please follow same resolution.

[WORKAROUND]
In case of several CTNs that are first net for the same BAN, remove the first
net indicator to all in subscriber table. It is expected that all have the same
first net type on all subscribers.

@fn2banlvl
Script to move the FN indicator from CTN level to BAN level  WR #4430466
Please enter BAN: 337251440729
Check FAN_CUST_TYPE,FAN_CUST_SUB_TYPE on billing_account (FN=FirstNet | NULL=No FN)
old   1: select BAN,FAN_CUST_TYPE,FAN_CUST_SUB_TYPE,fan_id from billing_account where ban=&ban
new   1: select BAN,FAN_CUST_TYPE,FAN_CUST_SUB_TYPE,fan_id from billing_account where ban=337251440729

             BAN|FAN_CUST_T|FAN_CUST_S|FAN_ID
----------------|----------|----------|--------
    337251440729|          |          |60712373

1 row selected.

check fn_ind and fn_type from subscriber table
old   1: select customer_ban, subscriber_no,fn_ind,fn_type from subscriber where customer_ban=&ban
new   1: select customer_ban, subscriber_no,fn_ind,fn_type from subscriber where customer_ban=337251440729

    CUSTOMER_BAN|SUBSCRIBER_NO       |F|FN_TYPE
----------------|--------------------|-|----------
    337251440729|6199638360          |Y|V1

1 row selected.

specify the CTN which FN level will be moved to BAN level
Please enter CTN/Subscriber_No(in): 6199638360
old   1: update billing_account set FAN_CUST_TYPE='FN',FAN_CUST_SUB_TYPE=(select fn_type from subscriber where customer_ban=&ban and subscriber_no=&ctn) where ban=&ban
new   1: update billing_account set FAN_CUST_TYPE='FN',FAN_CUST_SUB_TYPE=(select fn_type from subscriber where customer_ban=337251440729 and subscriber_no=6199638360) where ban=337251440729

1 row updated.

old   1: update subscriber set FN_ind=null,FN_type=null where subscriber_no in ('&ctn') and customer_id=&ban
new   1: update subscriber set FN_ind=null,FN_type=null where subscriber_no in ('6199638360') and customer_id=337251440729

1 row updated.

Check FAN_CUST_TYPE,FAN_CUST_SUB_TYPE on billing_account (FN=FirstNet | NULL=No FN)
old   1: select BAN,FAN_CUST_TYPE,FAN_CUST_SUB_TYPE,fan_id from billing_account where ban=&ban
new   1: select BAN,FAN_CUST_TYPE,FAN_CUST_SUB_TYPE,fan_id from billing_account where ban=337251440729

             BAN|FAN_CUST_T|FAN_CUST_S|FAN_ID

   File:  dcs_ accttp.c  Line:  11183    (dcs_ gt_ acc_ type)

[WORKAROUND]
1. In group level, subscriber 3378868740 does not have a llp tier associated to 
its assigned group. To get it populated, with below query we can identify
which socs would provide the missing tier

Select sa.llp_tier,sa.subscriber_no,sa.soc,sa.soc_effective_date,sa.effective_date,
sa.expiration_date,sa.rc_eff_rsn_code,sa.rc_exp_rsn_code,sa.service_type,sa.rel_soc,
sa.REL_SOC_SEQ_NO,sa.glpp_id,sa.srv_ftr_ind,sa.soc_seq_no,sa.soc_ver_no,
sa.agr_parking_ind,sa.agr_enabler_ind
from service_agreement sa, soc s where sa.ban=287274039172
and sa.soc=s.soc
and s.data_group_ind='P'
and sa.rc_eff_rsn_code='A'
and s.gen_attribute like '%LLP%'
and sa.rc_exp_rsn_code='Q'
order by expiration_date;

LLP_TIER|SUBSCRIBER_NO|SOC      |SOC_EFFEC|EFFECTIVE|EXPIRATIO|R|R|S|REL_SOC|REL_SOC_SEQ_NO|GLPP_ID|S| SOC_SEQ_NO|SOC_VER_NO|A|A
--------|-------------|---------|---------|---------|---------|-|-|-|-------|--------------|-------|-|-----------|----------|-|-
MID0001 |3378868740   |LLFA105B |17-APR-24|17-APR-24|13-MAY-25|A|Q|R|       |              |       |S|10063790174|         1| |
MID0001 |3378868740   |LLFA95B  |13-MAY-25|13-MAY-25|09-FEB-26|A|Q|R|       |              |       |S|10898394145|         2| |

2. Unexpire the most recent one. The price plan LLGUNLB should have one of those 
socs associated
create table sa_bkp_wr as select * from service_agreement
where ban=287274039172 and subscriber_no='3378868740' and soc='LLFA95B';
update service_agreement set expiration_date=null, rc_exp_rsn_code=null,
application_id='CSMT1'
where ban=287274039172 and subscriber_no='3378868740' and soc='LLFA95B';

3. Commit Changes and ask user to retry restore.
@c

[DESCRIPTION]

[ERROR]
Promo SOC

[DESCRIPTION]
Question: MO76836
I need clarification whether it is a SOC that is a discount against IDP charges,
or if it is intended to be a IDP SOC that should affect usage rating.  
When this SOC was added to this BAN, I see in the memo table "Adding Promotional
IDP soc for 50% off ATT Employee and Retire subscribers on Tablets and Smartphones."
If we can verify that this is only supposed to be a discount against IDP charges,
that would address BQ's concern.

BAN: 436105548807
CTN: 5102199605

We can see soc IDPPROATT is active since 02/13/2026 with feature GNDISP by Star Service.
    MEMO_BAN|   MEMO_ID|MEMO_DATE|MEMO|MEMO_SYSTEM_TXT                                                       |SYS_CREAT|SYS_UPDAT|OPERATOR_ID
------------|----------|---------|----|----------------------------------------------------------------------|---------|---------|-----------
436105548807|8086152071|06-JUN-22|1023|Subscriber level SOC created.  SOC: IRCNNOAUT.  Effective: 06/06/2022.|06-JUN-22|         |  190995860
436105548807|9538668402|13-FEB-26|1023|Subscriber level SOC created.  SOC: IDPPROATT.  Effective: 02/13/2026.|13-FEB-26|         |  193460985

  USER_ID|USER_SHORT_NAME|USER_FULL_NAME
---------|---------------|-----------------------
190995860|m97698         |STAR SERVICE CSI SYS ID

Document Searcher:
How the platform distinguishes the two possibilities (what to expect)
- If IDPPROATT is a promotional (discount / bolt‑on) SOC:
- Promo SOCs for IDP are recorded in the RLH_PROMOTION table and can override the
base daily fee for specific days, with configurable day limits and effective/expiration dates;
bolt‑on promos are identified by a promo attribute (e.g., GEN_ATTRIBUTE such as RLH_PRMO_BLT_ON)
and may be zero‑dollar promos that still appear on the bill via feature_code settings 
([PID308462]; see RLH_PROMOTION notes).
- Billing will prefer the promo rows (subject to day limits and promo priority)
and create promo‑fee charges for qualifying days; remaining days fall back to
the base SOC daily fee ([PID308462]).

How to interpret typical results (examples)
- Example A (promo SOC): RLH_PROMOTION row with PROMO_SOC = IDPPROATT, PROMO_FEE = 0,
DAY_LIMIT = 5, maps to RLH_BASE_SOC = AATIDP123 → IDPPROATT is a bolt‑on promo that gives
up to 5 free days against that base IDP offer during the promo period ([PID308462]).
- Example B (base IDP SOC): RLH_SOC_AND_FEE row for IDPPROATT with TIER_RATE_IND = 'Y'
and RLH_TIER_FEE rows for tier 1 = $10, tier 2 = $5 → IDPPROATT is a tiered IDP SOC
and rating will apply the tiered daily fees across devices on the same account/day ([PID323445]).
- Example C (non‑IDP or unrelated): No rows in RLH_PROMOTION, RLH_SOC_AND_FEE, or
RLH_TIER_FEE but exists in general SOC master as a different service type → IDPPROATT
is not acting as an IDP/promo SOC in the billing layer (must be investigated in its
owning product domain).

Answer:
If IDPPROATT is a promotional (discount / bolt‑on) SOC: Promo SOCs for IDP are recorded 
in the RLH_PROMOTION table and can override the base daily fee for specific days,
with configurable day limits and effective/expiration dates; bolt‑on promos are
identified by a promo attribute (e.g., GEN_ATTRIBUTE such as RLH_PRMO_BLT_ON)
and may be zero‑dollar promos.

soc_description,gen_attribute from SOC  where SOC='IDPPROATT';
